\ge like, similar

\xv astok
\xe until, while

likka taldok tɕʰak astik, cot
astik tsutsuna da!

a little bit (of things like) fodder and a
little bit (of things like) grass!

\lx bap
\a
\u
\ps v
\ge be forced to do
\pd -de
\ue
\ec WT 'bab, bab ~ babs, 'bab
\rf Jk. hirchum
\xv girok kudzumaŋ elde
bapdza.
\xe I was forced to go to Kullu. (TD)
\xv tʰadzui bonʈʰek handok
hoɕmei dzuknaŋ ɲampo
bete kinʑa bapipahendʑi
\xe For that reason you will give birth to
children suffering pain. WoL1.41
\xv gi tʰe len liktɕa bapdza.
\xe It was my duty to do this work.

\lx lik
\a
\u
\sn 1
\ps v
\ge do
\pd -tɕa
\ue
\ec -
\rf Jk. ligchum
\xv han kʰa liktɕek
\xe What are you doing?
\xv gi(zi) len liktɕek.
\xe I do work.
\xv gizi len likmen.
\xe I did work.
\xv gizi likte.
\xe I will do (work).
\xv han len le!
\xe Do work!
\xv han len liktela?
\xe Do you want to work?
\xv gi len maliktɕa!
\xe I don't want to work!
\xv hã, gi len likte!
\xe Yes, I want to work!
\xv hanzi likmen la?
\xe Did you do (this work)? (Asked by
Lama Paljosh when we come out of
the monastery and see some work that
has been done outside)
\xv han liktɕekla?
\xe Are you working? (Asked by Lama
Paljosh when coming out of the
monastery and seeing me doing some
work on the other side of the way.)
\xv han taruŋ (len) liktɕekla?
\xe Are you still working? (Asked by L.P.
when coming out of the monastery and
seeing me doing some work and
knowing that I had already been
working there before.)
\xv ja tal ɲamatsʰi liktsʰa.
\xe Yesterday they did work.
\xv ja han ɲamatsʰi ligmenla?
\xe Did you work yesterday?
\xv hã, ja hiŋ ɲama tsʰaitsʰi
likmen.
\xe Yes, we all did work together
yesterday.
\np
\ng cEA
\ns
\nt
\so ZC
\dt 30/Jun/2013

\sn 2
\ps v
\ge draw
\pd -tɕa
\ue
\ec -
\rf
\xv gi mentok liktɕek.
\xe I' am drawing a flower.
\np
\ng cEA

\nt
\so ZC

(I am telling it to the cook at Khardang
Gompa)
\xv kʰardaŋ gompei zamen
neme niː.
\xe The food at Kharang Gompa is tasty.
(I'm telling it as an experience to some
other person (NOT in Khardang
Gompa)). > L.P. erklärt es als "past".
\np
\ng
\ns
\nt
\so ZC
\dt 30/Jun/2013

\lx tʰaŋ
\a
\u  
\ps v
\ge see
\pd -tɕa
\ue
\ec WT mthong
\rf
\xv gidzi tal bazardok tʰaŋmen.
\xe I saw him a the market.
\xv gidzi tal tʰaŋtɕek.
\xe I seem him. (SA)
\xv talzi girok tʰaŋtɕare.
\xe He is seeing me. (SA)
\xv gidzi la tʰaŋtɕare.
\xe I see a mountain. (TD)
\xv hanzi tʰeimaŋ cum
tʰaŋmenla? - gidzi ma tʰaŋǃ
\xe Can you see the house up there? - No,
I cannot see itǃ
\xv talzi girok bazardok
tʰaŋtak.
\xe He must have seen me at the market.
\xv talzi girok bazardok tʰaŋza.
\xe He saw me at the market.
\xv girok taldok bazardok
tʰaŋmen.
\xe I saw him at the market.
\xv talzi girok tʰaŋtɕare.
\xe He is looking at me.
\xv gidzi tʰaŋmen talzi tʰazurok
ɖawa daza.
\xe I saw that the gave her money.
